function extend(a) {
    if (1 == arguments.length) return a;
    for (var b = 1; b < arguments.length; b++) {
        var c = arguments[b];
        for (var d in c) c.hasOwnProperty(d) && (a[d] = c[d])
    }
    return a
}

function forEach(a, b, c) {
    if (a.forEach) a.forEach(b, c);
    else
        for (var d = 0; d < a.length; d++) b.call(c, a[d], d, a)
}

function overrideMethod(a, b, c) {
    var d = a[b] || function() {},
        e = function() {
            return d.apply(a, arguments)
        };
    a[b] = c(e)
}

function delegateMethod(a, b, c) {

    a[c] = function() {
        var e = b,
            f = b[c];

}

function escapeRegExp(a) {

function hasClass(a, b) {

}

function filterByClass(a, b, c) {
    for (var d = [], e = 0; e < a.length; e++) hasClass(a[e], b) == c && d.push(a[e]);

}

        function Tc(a) {

                if (c.forEach(ue), d = c[0], d.x = -d.r, d.y = 0, b(d), j > 1 && (e = c[1], e.x = e.r, e.y = 0, b(e), j > 2))

                        xe(d, e, f = c[g]);
                        var o = 0,
                            p = 1,
                            q = 1;
                        for (h = e._pack_next; h !== e; h = h._pack_next, p++)
                            if (se(h, f)) {
                                o = 1;
                                break

                    s = (m + n) / 2,
                    t = 0;
                for (g = 0; j > g; g++) f = c[g], f.x -= r, f.y -= s, t = Math.max(t, f.r + Math.sqrt(f.x * f.x + f.y * f.y));
                a.r = t, c.forEach(ve)
            }

        function xe(a, b, c) {

                e = b.x - a.x,
                f = b.y - a.y;

                    h = e * e + f * f;
                g *= g, d *= d;
                var i = .5 + (d - g) / (2 * h),
                    j = Math.sqrt(Math.max(0, 2 * g * (d + h) - (d -= h) * d - g * g)) / (2 * h);
                c.x = a.x + i * e + j * f, c.y = a.y + i * f - j * e
            } else c.x = a.x + d, c.y = a.y
        }

        function mf(a, b, c, d, e) {
            var f = a[0] - b[0],
                g = a[1] - b[1],
                h = (e ? d : -d) / Math.sqrt(f * f + g * g),
                i = h * g,
                j = -h * f,
                k = a[0] + i,
                l = a[1] + j,
                m = b[0] + i,
                n = b[1] + j,
                o = (k + m) / 2,
                p = (l + n) / 2,
                q = m - k,
                r = n - l,
                s = q * q + r * r,
                t = c - d,
                u = k * n - m * l,
                v = (0 > r ? -1 : 1) * Math.sqrt(t * t * s - u * u),
                w = (u * r - q * v) / s,
                x = (-u * q - r * v) / s,
                y = (u * r + q * v) / s,
                z = (-u * q + r * v) / s,
                A = w - o,
                B = x - p,
                C = y - o,
                D = z - p;
            return A * A + B * B > C * C + D * D && (w = y, x = z), [
                [w - i, x - j],
                [w * c / t, x * c / t]
            ]
        }

        function wf(a, b) {
            if (b.length < 1 || a.length != b.length && a.length != b.length + 2) return of(a);

            }
